@USHouseHistory President Ronald Reagan’s State of the Union address for 1986 was rescheduled to February 4th from January 28 because of the Challenger disaster that took place earlier in the day. https://t.co/pt5ffXlxkj
Presidents who delivered their annual message (officially known as the State of the Union Address since 1947) in person to Congress via @USHouseHistory https://t.co/f1n2qQwue7
Jimmy Carter was the last President to deliver his State of the Union Address (his final one) to Congress only in writing January 16,1981:		"To the Congress of the United States: The State of the Union is sound. Our economy is recovering from a recession." https://t.co/KVzqcGCUEC
Pelosi notes US Constitution only calls for the President to “from time to time give to the Congress Information of the State of the Union.” During 19th Century &amp; up until presidency of Woodrow Wilson,these annual State of the Union messages were delivered to Congress in writing.
